class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eAgents and Agentic flows\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-agents-and-agentic-flows\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Agents and Agentic flows\" href=\"#agents-and-agentic-flows\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAgents are AI systems that can:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake decisions about what actions to take\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse tools to accomplish tasks\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMaintain state and context\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLearn from previous interactions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWork towards specific goals\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAgentic flow is not necessarily a completely independent agent,\nbut it can still make some decisions during the flow execution\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eA typical agentic flow consists of:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eReceiving a user request\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAnalyzing the request and available tools\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDeciding on the next action\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eExecuting the action using appropriate tools\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEvaluating the results\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEither completing the task or continuing with more actions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe key difference from basic RAG is that agents can:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake multiple search queries\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCombine information from different sources\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDecide when to stop searching\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse their own knowledge when appropriate\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eChain multiple actions together\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSo in agentic RAG, the system\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ehas access to the history of previous actions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003emakes decisions independently based on the current information\nand the previous actions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eLet's implement this step by step.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eMaking RAG more agentic\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca more \"agentic\":\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTell the LLM that it can answer the question directly or look up context\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProvide output class=\"pl-en\"\u003eprint\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eprompt\u003c/span\u003e)\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eHere, \u003ccode\u003ebuild_context\u003c/code\u003e is a helper function from the previous\ncode:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def build_context(search_results):\n    context = \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n\n    for doc in search_results:\n        context = context + f\u0026quot;section: {doc['section']}\\nquestion: {doc['question']}\\nanswer: {doc['text']}\\n\\n\u0026quot;\n\n    return context.strip()\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"answer = llm(prompt)\nprint(answer)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eanswer\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePart 2: Agentic search\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-part-2-agentic-search\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Part 2: Agentic search\" href=\"#part-2-agentic-search\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSo far we had two actions only: search and answer.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBut we can let our \"agent\" formulate one or more\nsearch queries - and do it for a few iterations until\nwe found an answer\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eLet's build a prompt:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eList available actions:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSearch in FAQ\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAnswer using own knowledge\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAnswer using information extracted from FAQ\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProvide access to the previous actions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHave clear stop criteria (no more than X iterations)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWe also specify the output format, so it's easier to parse it\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"prompt_template = \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\nYou're a course teaching assistant.\n\nYou're given a QUESTION from a course student and that you need to answer with your own knowledge and provided CONTEXT.\n\nThe CONTEXT is build with the documents from our FAQ database.\nSEARCH_QUERIES contains the queries that were used to retrieve the documents\nfrom FAQ to and add them to the context.\nPREVIOUS_ACTIONS contains the actions you already performed.\n\nAt the beginning the CONTEXT is empty.\n\nYou can perform the following actions:\n\n- Search in the FAQ database to get more data for the CONTEXT\n- Answer the question using the CONTEXT\n- Answer the question using your own knowledge\n\nFor the SEARCH action, build search requests based on the CONTEXT and the QUESTION.\nCarefully analyze the CONTEXT and generate the requests to deeply explore the topic. \n\nDon't use search queries used at the previous iterations.\n\nDon't repeat previously performed actions.\n\nDon't perform more than {max_iterations} iterations for a given student question.\nThe current iteration number: {iteration_number}. If we exceed the allowed number \nof iterations, give the best possible answer with the provided information.\n\nOutput templates:\n\nIf you want to perform search, use this template:\n\n{{\n\u0026quot;action\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;SEARCH\u0026quot;,\n\u0026quot;reasoning\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;\u0026lt;add your reasoning here\u0026gt;\u0026quot;,\n\u0026quot;keywords\u0026quot;: [\u0026quot;search query 1\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;search query 2\u0026quot;, ...]\n}}\n\nIf you can answer the QUESTION using CONTEXT, use this template:\n\n{{\n\u0026quot;action\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;ANSWER_CONTEXT\u0026quot;,\n\u0026quot;answer\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;\u0026lt;your answer\u0026gt;\u0026quot;,\n\u0026quot;source\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;CONTEXT\u0026quot;\n}}\n\nIf the context doesn't contain the answer, use your own knowledge to answer the question\n\n{{\n\u0026quot;action\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;ANSWER\u0026quot;,\n\u0026quot;answer\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;\u0026lt;your answer\u0026gt;\u0026quot;,\n\u0026quot;source\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;OWN_KNOWLEDGE\u0026quot;\n}}\n\n\u0026lt;QUESTION\u0026gt;\n{question}\n\u0026lt;/QUESTION\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;SEARCH_QUERIES\u0026gt;\n{search_queries}\n\u0026lt;/SEARCH_QUERIES\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;CONTEXT\u0026gt; \n{context}\n\u0026lt;/CONTEXT\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;PREVIOUS_ACTIONS\u0026gt;\n{previous_actions}\n\u0026lt;/PREVIOUS_ACTIONS\u0026gt;\n\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;.strip()\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eprompt_template\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eYou're a course teaching assistant.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eYou're given a QUESTION from a course student and that you need to answer with your own knowledge and provided CONTEXT.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eThe CONTEXT is build with the documents from our FAQ database.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eSEARCH_QUERIES contains the queries that were used to retrieve the documents\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003efrom FAQ to and add them to the context.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003ePREVIOUS_ACTIONS contains the actions you already performed.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eAt the beginning the CONTEXT is empty.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eYou can perform the following actions:\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e- Search in the FAQ database to get more data for the CONTEXT\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e- Answer the question using the CONTEXT\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e- Answer the question using your own knowledge\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eFor the SEARCH action, build search requests based on the CONTEXT and the QUESTION.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eCarefully analyze the CONTEXT and generate the requests to deeply explore the topic. \u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eDon't use search queries used at the previous iterations.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eDon't repeat previously performed actions.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eDon't perform more than {max_iterations} iterations for a given student question.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eThe current iteration number: {iteration_number}. If we exceed the allowed number \u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eof iterations, give the best possible answer with the provided information.\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eOutput templates:\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eIf you want
